GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(v) - omega0**c0*(gamma*Abs(v)**c1 + c2)*x
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed) is
\[
-3.4278620084\,x\,(0.03499775369|v|^{1/3}+1)\;+\;0.1002992557\sin t\;-\;0.8884946707\sin v.
\]
So it has three essential structures:

1) a **linear-in-\(x\)** term whose coefficient is \(-(A|v|^{1/3}+B)\) with \(A,B\neq 0\) (so it is \(x\) times a **non-polynomial** function of \(|v|\), specifically \(|v|^{1/3}\)),  
2) a **pure \(\sin(t)\)** term (no \(x\) factor),  
3) a **pure \(\sin(v)\)** term (no \(x\) factor, and depends on \(v\) trigonometrically, not algebraically).

Any candidate must be able (possibly after setting some constants to 0 and using a plausible domain restriction like \(v\ge 0\)) to reproduce all three.

**GT:** `-3.42786200841899*x*(0.034997753689396*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 1) + 0.100299255716928*sin(t) - 0.888494670723871*sin(v)`

Expanding: `-3.42786200841899*x - 0.119969938498498*x*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 0.100299255716928*sin(t) - 0.888494670723871*sin(v)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `x` (linear in x)
2. `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` (x times cube root of |v|)
3. `sin(t)`
4. `sin(v)`

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*exp(c1*x) + c2*exp(c3*x)*exp(c4*v) + c5*exp(c6*x)*sin(c7*t + c8) + c9*x`
Contains exponentials in x and v, sin(t) modulated by exp(x). Cannot produce `sin(v)` or `x*Abs(v)^(1/3)`. Setting c1=c3=c6=0: `c0 + c2*exp(c4*v) + c5*sin(c7*t+c8) + c9*x`. Still no sin(v) or x*|v|^(1/3).
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0 + c1*x + c2*log(c3*exp(c4*v) + 1) + c5*sin(c6*t + c7)`
Has x, log(softplus of v), sin(t). No `x*Abs(v)^(1/3)` or `sin(v)`. log(c3*exp(c4*v)+1) cannot equal sin(v) for all v.

**Candidate 4:** `c0*x³ + c1*x² + c2*v*x² + c3*x + c4 + c5*v + c6*x*cos(c7*t) + c8*x*cos(c9*t)`
Polynomial in x,v plus x*cos(t) terms. No sin(v), no x*|v|^(1/3). x*cos(t) ≠ sin(t).
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** Like Candidate 1 without the linear x term. Same issues.
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `c0 + c1*exp(c2*x) + c3*v*Abs(v) + c4*sin(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*Abs(v)**c8`
Setting c1=0 (c2=0 gives constant): `c0 + c3*v*|v| + c4*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7*v*|v|^c8`. Note v*|v|^c8 = sign(v)*|v|^(c8+1). No x term, no sin(v).
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]
